Robberies Recorded 167

Around 9:30 AM yesterday morning, two thugs, one wielding a knife and the other a pistol, broke into No. 1895 Yangshupu Road and ordered everyone to remain silent. They robbed clothes and ornaments worth 200 yuan.

At No. 3404 Zhoujiazui Road, Zhoujiazui Road, Hudong, around 6:00 AM yesterday morning, four bandits rushed in, all armed with pistols. They dragged the homeowner out of bed, pointed their guns at his chest, and forced him to hand over the keys. They ransacked the house. One person committed the robbery for an hour before leaving. According to statistics, they robbed gold jewelry, precious stones, fox fur, etc., estimated to be worth more than 1,000 yuan.

Lion Brand Universal Oil Trademark Revoked 168

Hu Wenhu, owner of Tiger Brand Yong An Tang, invented various effective medicines including Universal Oil, which have long been registered and filed. However, a certain pharmacy mixed and sold a Lion Brand Universal Oil in an attempt to profit illegally. Tiger Brand Yong An Tang filed a complaint with the Guangdong government and requested the Trademark Bureau to assess and handle the matter. According to the Trademark Bureau's assessment document No. 16, the Lion Brand Universal Oil was clearly counterfeit and violated the trademark law. Therefore, registration No. 9195 for the Lion Brand trademark was revoked.

Lost Boy Awaiting Claim 169

The Municipal Public Security Bureau reported yesterday that a lost boy named Jiang Qicai was sent by the First Precinct of the First District. According to the boy, he is ten years old and from Haimen County. His home is in Shirun Kang Town, Haimen. His sister-in-law manages the household affairs at home. His brother, named Ji Hong, works as a clerk in a cigarette paper shop in Shanghai. He was an apprentice in a shop that makes bodhi prayer beads. He went out to play and got lost. He doesn't know the address of his brother's shop or the shop where he is an apprentice. The boy has been transferred to Xin Puyu Tang to be cared for while awaiting claim.

Weather Report 170

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the sky over the Shandong coast and the Yangtze River basin would be mostly cloudy. The southern coast would be overcast with rain. The northeast wind over the Yellow Sea and East China Sea would strengthen. A hurricane in the Pacific Ocean is moving northwest, so the weather around northern Luzon is bad. Also, the temperature in this city in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday was a high of 76.8 and a low of 55.0. On the same day last year, the high was 89.8 and the low was 65.2.

Letter 171

To the Editor,

We are writing to inform you that the Bureau of Finance collects house tax at a rate of 10% for residential households and 14% for commercial establishments, regardless of whether they are Chinese or foreign, without discrimination. Recently, we read in the local news section of your newspaper on the 22nd that foreign residents in Zhabei pay house tax, and the Bureau of Finance has officially announced that from the summer tax collection onwards, both residential households and commercial establishments will be charged at a rate of 10%. This is a rumor and is inaccurate. We request that you correct this as soon as possible to avoid misunderstandings.

Sincerely,

The North Shanghai Tax Collection Office of the Shanghai Special Municipal Bureau of Finance

May 24th

May 25, 1930 (Shen Bao, Fifth Edition) Sunday (17)

Shen Bao Education News

Special Issue No. 2 of the Ninth Far Eastern Games 172

First Day of the Far Eastern Games

Grand Opening in Tokyo Yesterday, Stirring the Entire City

Athletes from Four Countries Begin Competing for Titles

Chinese Baseball Team Defeats the Philippines 9-6

Chinese Women's Volleyball Team Defeats the Philippines 2-0

Chinese Basketball Team Unfortunate Defeat to Japan

Chinese and Philippine Women's Tennis Teams Each Win a Singles Match

1500-Meter, Long Jump, and High Jump Set World Records

Liu Changchun's Injured Foot Has Not Healed; Eliminated in the 400-Meter Preliminary

Wang Zhengting's Eulogy Included in the Order of Ceremony After Negotiation

Grand Opening Yesterday

The Venue Was Extremely Lively

With a Total of 60,000 People

(Special dispatch from our Tokyo office on the 24th) Today marks the opening of the ninth Far Eastern Games. Flags are flying throughout Tokyo, and the residents are all elated and excited, with the whole country in a frenzy. The competition venue in the outer garden of Meiji Jingu is brilliantly decorated. The flags of the countries participating in the Games flutter in the sky. Spectators, both men and women, are shoulder to shoulder, with no fewer than 60,000 people. Despite the large size of the venue, it was completely packed. At noon, Prime Minister Hamaguchi, government officials, and the diplomatic corps arrived one after another.

Chinese Team Parade 173

Li Guochen and Lu Ming Carry the National Flag at the Front

Circling the Venue While Military Music Plays and the Games Song Is Sung

(Dispatch from our Tokyo office on the 24th) At the twelfth chime, a signal cannon fired, and the military band led the committee members and athletes from the four countries into the venue. The Chinese athletes were at the front, with Li Guochen carrying the Blue Sky White Sun national flag, leading the team. Lu Ming carried the Physical Education Promotion Association flag behind him, with two female athletes assisting on either side. Then came the officials, followed by the female athletes from the track and field, volleyball, and swimming teams, and the male athletes from the track and field, soccer, swimming, tennis, and basketball teams, in that order. Following the Chinese athletes were the Philippine athletes, then the Indian athletes, and finally the Japanese athletes, in the same order. As the athletes circled the venue, the audience applauded and cheered, their voices like thunder. Then, the athletes lined up in front of the command platform. The Japanese military band played national music, and many spectators took off their hats and stood up, singing in harmony. After the music, Vice-President Tanaka, the Minister of Education, read the imperial edict from Prince Chichibu, followed by eulogies and welcoming speeches from various parties.

The Chinese Baseball Team That Defeated the Philippines Yesterday

President Kishi Delivers a Speech 174

(Dispatch from our Tokyo office on the 24th) President Kishi Kiyoshi delivered the opening speech, saying, "Today, we are opening the ninth Games, and we are very pleased to have athletes from four countries joining us. We hope for excellent results and to strengthen international relations," and so on.

President Chichibu's Speech 175

(Read by Vice-President Tanaka)

We Are Delighted to See India's Participation

We Hope the Athletes Are Fair, Humble, Loving, and Friendly

(United Press dispatch from Tokyo on the 24th) Prince Chichibu issued an imperial edict, which was read by Vice-President Tanaka, the Minister of Education:

"Now we open the ninth Far Eastern Games. This Games, according to the organization of this association, has gradually grown and become grander with the mutual trust and cooperation of people from various countries. Today, we are even more pleased to see the participation of India. We hope that all of you will embody the spirit of this Games, and while using your bodies and skills honed in peacetime to compete to the best of your ability, we hope that you will always maintain a sense of fairness, humility, love, and friendship, and demonstrate the spirit of sportsmanship to promote the friendship of friendly nations."

The Chinese Women's Volleyball Team That Defeated the Philippines Yesterday

Prime Minister Hamaguchi's Congratulatory Speech 176

(United Press dispatch from Tokyo on the 24th) The congratulatory speech from Prime Minister Hamaguchi at the opening ceremony of the Far Eastern Games (read by Secretary-General Suzuki) is as follows:

"We are delighted that the ninth Far Eastern Games are being held in our country. Since its founding, this Games has been enriched in content and improved in form over the years, and it has become very prosperous. Moreover, we are honored that athletes and committee members from India, in addition to our long-time friendly nations of China and the Philippines, have come from afar to participate this time. We sincerely hope that under the leadership of Prince Chichibu, all of you will do your best in competition and strive for supremacy, so as to achieve the purpose of the Games." (signed) Hamaguchi Bokō, Prime Minister of the Cabinet

The Philippine Women's Volleyball Players Defeated by China

Chinese Representative 177

Zhang Boling's Speech

Hoping the Games Will Produce Excellent Records

(United Press dispatch from Tokyo on the 24th) Chinese representative Zhang Boling gave a speech, the main points of which are as follows: "I have the honor to represent the National Sports Advancement Association of China and to express my hope for the success of this Games and offer my congratulations. Since arriving in the East, we have received the greatest welcome from the Japanese organizing committee and the Japanese people, for which we are extremely grateful. The Games have been held nine times, and this is the third time in Japan. The thoroughness of the preparations and the grandeur of the scale surpass those of previous Games. I sincerely hope that this Games will produce many excellent records, and that on this occasion, all participating representatives will promote the spirit of sportsmanship and the idea of friendship and closeness."

Philippine Representative 178

Vargas's Speech

Far Eastern Nationalities' Intimacy

(United Press dispatch from Tokyo on the 24th) Philippine representative Vargas's speech was roughly as follows: "The athletes from the Philippines have come, and this beautiful Japan hopes for the greatest success in the history of the Far Eastern Games in the following two respects: One is to enhance the international intimacy of the Far Eastern nationalities, and the other is to declare at home and abroad that Far Eastern athletes, under the guidance of Japan, will compete against athletes from other countries and nationalities."

Indian Representative 179

Mukherjee's Speech

Demanding a Proper Place in the Far East

(United Press dispatch from Tokyo on the 24th) Indian representative Mukherjee's speech was roughly as follows: "The ninth Far Eastern Games, India's first participation, has two major significance: one is that India is now demanding a proper place among the Far Eastern nationalities, and the other is that India is sending athletes to convey the Indian spirit and peaceful goodwill and friendship to the athletes of the other three countries."

The ceremony was completed, and it was already one chime past. Athletes from each country then withdrew.

Wang Zhengting's Eulogy Included in the Order of Ceremony 182

Japanese Sports Association Discusses Late into the Night

Negotiation Resolved by Acting Representative Jiang

(Dispatch from our Tokyo office on the 24th) Regarding the issue of Honorary President Dr. Wang Zhengting's eulogy, after our country protested, the Executive Committee of the Japanese Sports Association held a meeting last night, lasting until 11:30 PM. The final decision was to include it in the order of ceremony, with Acting Representative Jiang from our country's embassy in Japan reading it. It is said that this issue has caused serious comments from all sides.

Prepared by Asahi and Nichinichi Newspapers

The Chinese Team Showed Good Spirits After Entering

(Dispatch from our Tokyo office on the 24th) This time, both the Asahi Shimbun and the Nichinichi Shimbun have airplanes prepared, circling the sky above the venue. The order throughout the venue has always been very strict, and the Chinese athletes have shown very good spirits, it is said.

Yesterday's Competition Situation

Men's Baseball Championship 184

The Chinese Baseball Team Makes a Splash in the Far East

Defeats the Philippines 9-6 Yesterday

(Dispatch from our Tokyo office on the 24th) The Chinese baseball team surprisingly defeated the Philippines with stunning skills in the first competition of the Games yesterday. The result was 9-6. Thousands of spectators were full of praise, and Japan felt particularly apprehensive, fearing that it would follow the same path as the Philippines. Chinese pitcher Cheng Bingguan performed well in the first four innings, preventing the opposing side from advancing. In the fifth, sixth, and seventh innings, he weakened slightly, losing five points. From the eighth inning onwards, Zhong You replaced him and also had good results. Catcher Cai Yunping was steady and reliable. Philippine pitcher Naibalv took the field and performed unfavorably, so he was switched with right fielder Shan Dousi. Neither of them showed any special strengths. Replacement catcher Sha Beilong. The competition situation is as follows:

A Head-On Blow 185

The Philippines took the field first, retreated unfavorably. Zhang Rongan hit the ball and occupied second base, shocking the whole stadium. The Philippine pitcher's face showed panic. Lu Shujie's sacrifice hit allowed Zhang to advance to third base. Feng Yuhe took the field to take the lead. Zhang Rongan flew back to home base and scored the first point. Cai Yunping hit a safe hit and advanced to third base, and Feng also followed him back to home base. Seeing the dangerous situation, the Philippines immediately changed the pitcher, replaced by Shan Dousi. Both sides held each other firmly, and there was no disturbance.

Danger Everywhere 186

The Chinese pitcher used skillful curve balls, making it difficult for the opposing side to gain any ground in the first four innings. In the fifth inning, the defense was careless, and the Philippines regained one point. In the sixth inning, the Philippines scored another point, but China scored two points. At this time, the situation between the two sides gradually became close. In the seventh inning, the Chinese shortstop made a mistake, and the Philippines ran back two runners. The scoreboard showed 5-5, and the spectators were worried for China.

Final Success 187

Fortunately, our country's athletes were veteran players with long experience. They did not panic and scored four points on the spot in the seventh inning. Those who returned to home base were Feng Yuhe, Cai Yunping, Yang Dongzhao, and Cheng Guanbing. In the eighth inning, the Philippines came on strong, fully occupying third base, but ultimately failed to achieve their goal and failed. In the ninth inning, the Philippines scored another point. As a result, China won 9-6.

Men's Basketball Championship

Chinese Basketball Team Unfortunately Loses to Japan 190

The Result Was 24-39

Japanese Referees Were Too Unfair

Continuously and Unjustifiably Penalizing Our Chinese Team

(Dispatch from our Tokyo office on the 24th) At 7:00 PM today, the first basketball match was a contest between China and Japan. More than 10,000 spectators sat on the grass. At that time, the cool breeze was gentle, the weather was very good, and all the conditions were very suitable. Almost all of the Chinese cheerleading team also arrived at the venue, because, based on past results, everyone thought that China would easily win. Who knew that the result would be beyond expectations, with a crushing defeat of 24-39. In the first three minutes, our country was penalized four times, allowing Japan to score two points. Later, a Japanese player scored another point. By seven minutes, our Yao Enhan finally made two baskets. However, our athletes, feeling indignant at being repeatedly penalized without reason, lost morale and their fighting spirit was greatly reduced. The basketball match could not be played as desired, and ultimately, the first half ended with the Japanese winning 15-12. In the second half, although they tried to cheer up and fight hard, hoping to reverse the situation, the surrounding shouts were too loud, disrupting the team members. Although several players were replaced, there was no progress, and our team lost again 12-24. In short, the referees in this competition were biased towards the Japanese side, so the Japanese team had the advantage everywhere. Their victory can be said to have been aided by the referees. Such unfair refereeing is really unprecedented for our national athletes. If all the competitions in this Games are like this, not only our team but also the Philippine team will probably have no hope of winning any titles.

May 25, 1930 (Shen Bao, Fifth Edition) Sunday (18)

Men's Volleyball Championship

The Philippines Defeats Japan 2-0 195

First Set 21-18

Second Set 21-14

(Dispatch from our Tokyo office on the 24th) In the men's volleyball championship match between Japan and the Philippines, from 3:00 PM onwards, the two sides fought fiercely in the first set. Both sides attacked and defended, advancing and retreating repeatedly. Their volleyball skills were excellent. The result was 21-18, with the Philippines winning. In the second set, the Japanese team played very fiercely at the beginning, winning with surprise attacks. The Philippines also took advantage of the opportunities to counterattack, putting all their effort into responding. The skill of their volleyball techniques was truly rare. After the two sides each scored 11 points, they switched sides. The Philippines attacked even more fiercely, and the Japanese team gradually felt exhausted and made little progress. The final result was 21-14, with the Philippines winning by a large margin. As a result, the Philippines defeated Japan 2-0.

Women's Volleyball Exhibition

China Defeats the Philippines 2-0 196

First Set 21-7

Second Set 21-17

(Dispatch from our Tokyo office on the 24th) The women's volleyball exhibition between China and the Philippines began at 1:30 PM. In the first set, our country's athletes were invincible, defeating the enemy as if taking something out of a pocket. The result was 21-7, with the Philippines suffering a crushing defeat. In the second set, the Philippine team became stronger, but our country's players were not weak either, fighting very fiercely. The third row defended the ball effectively. The result was another victory for China 21-17. However, the difference in this set was only four points. China ultimately won 2-0.

Liu Changchun Not Selected 206

Participated in the 100-Meter Preliminary

Injury Not Fully Healed, Resulting in Failure

Our Tokyo dispatch on the 24th: Our country's sprint athlete Liu Changchun suffered a hamstring injury, withdrew from the 100-meter and 200-meter races. He also failed to qualify in yesterday's 400-meter preliminary, which is a pity. Jiang Yunlong in the 1500-meter and Li Zhongsan in the high jump tried their best, but still did not score.

He was penalized for false starts twice, and started behind the others on the third start, unable to catch up. He dropped to fourth place, leading to his elimination.

Indian Flag Issue 208

Indian Residents Issue a Declaration Yesterday

Believing the Use of the British Flag Is Inappropriate

Compromise Solution Adopted

Our Tokyo dispatch on the 24th: Local Indian residents issued a declaration regarding the national flag issue, stating that although the Japan Sports Association has decided to use the British flag, they believe that even if political issues are put aside, this move is still inappropriate. It also said that the Indian athletes came to the East to participate only to show the Indian people's emphasis on sports, and do not represent the entire country of India.

Reuters, Tokyo, 24th: At the opening of the Far Eastern Games today, athletes from various countries entered the stadium following their flag bearers. The Indian flag adopted a compromise solution. Although it was in the style of the Indian Viceroy's flag, the pattern was divided into red, blue, and white to show obedience to the Kuomintang.

Athletes Discuss Their Strengths 213

United Press, Tokyo, 24th:

Chinese Chinese track and field athlete Lu Ming said to reporters, "The Chinese team's greatest hopes are Liu Changchun in the short distances, Jiang Yunlong in the 1500 meters, and Zhang Lingjia in the discus throw and decathlon."

Philippine track and field team leader Deribio said, "Atadar's leg injury has not healed, and his middle-distance results are not optimistic. However, Shintagaka in the short distances and Aranbura in the 400 meters have good results. In other competitions, we will have to fight hard. I hope all our team members have the determination to do their best."

Japanese Japanese basketball team captain Nomura Hitomi said, "The Japanese basketball team has lost every time, so we must avenge ourselves this time. We were ashamed to lose to the Philippine team by three points in Shanghai in the past. However, this time the formation of the Japanese team is the most complete ever. We will definitely win glory for the country and avenge our humiliation."

The athletes all looked very satisfied and lively, showing no signs of fatigue from the long journey. They were all wearing white flannel uniforms, with eye-catching badges on their chests. Staff members and athletes exchanged greetings with the welcomers for half an hour, then gathered in front of the station and boarded cars to their residences (female athletes stayed at the YWCA, male athletes stayed at the Japan Youth Hall).

Shanghai Volleyball Association Begins Registration 220

Deadline May 30th

Competition Begins in Early June

The Shanghai Volleyball Association is organized by the Chinese Athletic Federation. The regulations are as follows:

1. This association is organized by the Chinese National Athletic Federation.

2. The purpose of this association is to promote amateur sports and improve volleyball skills. 3. All Shanghai Chinese and Western schools and amateur sports organizations may join this association's competition.

3. This association consists of a committee of five members appointed by the Chinese National Athletic Federation to handle all association affairs. When necessary, the committee may convene a temporary general meeting to handle it.

4. If there are any protests from each team, a formal letter of protest should be sent to the secretariat within two days after the incident occurred, and submitted to the committee for resolution. Each protest must be accompanied by a deposit of five yuan. If the committee believes that the protest has sufficient grounds, the deposit of five yuan will be returned. If the committee denies it, the committee's decision will be the final judgment.

5. The penalties for violations of this association's regulations will be determined based on the severity of the violation, divided into (A) cancellation of the qualifications of the entire team and individuals, (B) suspension of the right to compete for individuals and the entire team, and (C) warning.

6. Each team will be issued 15 ball passes by this association to enter the venue.

7. A registration fee of two yuan must be paid at the time of registration.

8. If the committee considers an individual player unqualified, it may refuse their registration, but must publicize the reasons.

9. The competition will be conducted according to the rules set by the Far Eastern Games.

10. The competition schedule will be determined by this association. The competition locations will be at the athletic field on Labor Father Road. In case of rain, it will be changed to the basketball room.

11. Referees for the competition will be appointed by the Chinese Referees Association.

12. Each team must attend at the scheduled competition time. If there are special circumstances, a representative should be sent with a letter to the secretariat two days in advance to make arrangements.

13. Each time a team attends a competition, the captain must write out the real names of the participating team members and the serving order and hand it over to the referee at the time.

14. The two teams during the competition may each send a recorder and a line judge to assist the referee in performing their duties.

15. The competition time is from 4:30 PM every day, but on Saturdays and Sundays, it will be from 2:00 PM.

16. This competition is divided into Group A and Group B. When registering, each team must specify whether to join Group A or Group B. The champion team of each group will be given a prize by this association as a souvenir.

17. Depending on the number of registered teams, the competition will be a knockout or round-robin format.

18. The deadline for registration is May 30th, and the competition will begin in early June. The exact date will be announced later.

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau sent a letter to the Public Concession Ratepayers Association requesting assistance in the matter of recovering educational rights in the concessions. The reply from the association states: "In reply to your Bureau's letter No. 741 and the declaration on the recovery of educational rights in the concessions, we have read it carefully. The righteousness of the words is solemn and all Chinese people agree. Now, the recovery of the concessions has been listed by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs as an important task for this year and a special committee has been organized to plan it. If it can be realized as soon as possible, then all sovereignty will be fully recovered and fundamentally resolved. Our colleagues in this association are willing to make the greatest efforts to achieve this final goal. Before this is achieved, our association, organized by the Chinese citizens within the concessions, will spare no effort to do anything that is beneficial to the Chinese citizens. Education is a major plan for cultivating talents and is of particular importance. When the Chinese directors joined the Municipal Council in March of the 17th year, the first session of the representative conference decided on the proposals regarding the educational problems in the Public Concession, which were: 'The Chinese Education Committee must be organized by Chinese people as a principle, and the Chinese education expenses must be based on 20% of the tax revenue as a standard.' This association formally sent a letter to the board of directors of the Public Concession Municipal Council expressing its attitude. For the past three years, the Chinese directors and Chinese committee members have all been able to follow the resolutions of the representative conference and strive to expand Chinese education expenses within the possible range to suit the increase in schools for Chinese children, and have paid close attention to the management of Chinese educational rights. Although the principles and standards decided by the representative conference still require effort, we dare not slacken in the face of difficulties, and we dare not be complacent and forget the final goal. We have not neglected this matter in the slightest. As for the running dog race clubs and other places that harm customs, this association has criticized them all. The circumstances have been reviewed by the party. We are encouraged to renew our efforts, and this association will strive even harder to support them. This is addressed to the Director of the Shanghai Special Municipal Education Bureau, Chen, from the Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers Association.

A Wonderful Method of Repelling Bandits · Chen · Bo · Ying 229

The art of national martial arts is originally our country's specialty. Those who are particularly skilled often keep their skills secret and do not pass them on to others, resulting in a gradual decline. Now the government is promoting national martial arts and has set up special halls. From now on, the disciples of Wudang and Shaolin will have successors. Recently, I saw an anecdote recorded by the Old Man Juan Shi, which is extremely interesting. I quickly recorded it to share with readers. Mr. Zou Jingfu of Wuxi, named An Chang, was honest and upright. He studied books in his youth, and was skilled in playing the qin, calligraphy, and painting. His paintings resembled Wen Hengshan, and his calligraphy followed the style of Mi Fei. He was also proficient in arithmetic and understood Tianyuan Siyuan. In his later years, he called himself Weng, which meant borrowing one "yi" of books and returning one "yi" of books. He was thin and tall, and gentle and refined. Those who saw him did not know that he was skilled in martial arts. During the Taiping Rebellion, Mr. Zou was old. He took refuge in a certain town in the northwest of the county (seemingly Mount Hou). It faced water and was backed by mountains, with a bridge as the only passage. The place was remote and the population was quite large. One day, bandits suddenly arrived, and the whole town was shocked. Women were all crying. Mr. Zou said, "Don't be disturbed for now. Let me observe them. If those who come do not have firearms, there may still be a strategy to resist them." There was a willow tree in the square, about three zhang tall. Mr. Zou leaped to the top of it and looked around for a moment. He flew down and had a happy expression. He said to the crowd, "No harm done. The responsibility lies with this old man." He wanted a weapon. Someone presented him with a broadsword, which Mr. Zou broke like a broken gourd. He said, "This is useless." Several men carried an iron bar weighing over a hundred catties. Mr. Zou refused it and said, "Why use this to play with rats?" Suddenly, he saw a floor-scrubbing brush in the corner of the house. Its handle was made of white waxwood. It was like a half-section spear of Geshu. He smiled and said, "This is enough." He took it and removed the cloth strands, and took it out. There was a toilet on the road. He put the end of the pole in and soaked it. He came out and ground it in the soil so that it would not drip. He slowly walked to the other side of the bridge. After a while, the bandits arrived and shouted, "Old man, are you not afraid of death?" Mr. Zou slowly replied, "Rats jumping around, what a shame. If you want to cross this bridge, why not kill this old man?" The bandits were angry and thrust their spears forward. Mr. Zou raised the pole and made a circular motion. All the spears slipped from their hands and flew away. The bandits were even more angry and attacked with their blades. Mr. Zou calmly waved the pole, rotating it among the crowd. Before long, the bandits were all vomiting madly and fled. When waving the pole, he wiped the mouths of the bandits with the filthy end. The village was saved.

Record of a Famous Flower Revealing Spring's Splendor · Yín · Qí 230

An official in Wu County had fine peonies in his back garden. It was said that his family had moved them from Luoyang when he was an official there many years ago. Wei Purple and Yao Yellow, the most famous varieties. When they bloomed, guests came to admire them, and banquets were held. Everyone praised them, and some asked for cuttings. Even good friends were refused. A certain notable attempted to bribe the gardener, but the gardener declined, saying that the master's precautions were strict and there was no way to arrange it. Over time, people became jealous. A neighbor named Yang had a guest named Qian, who was extremely resourceful. Qian said to Yang, "Do you want to get the peonies from that official? I see that the flowers are lush and close to the garden wall, and the roots are likely to be growing under the wall and into your property, which is separated by only a wall. We can perform a procedure to lead the roots to your land. After a year or two, you will have a fine variety of this famous flower." Yang was delighted and asked how to perform the procedure. Qian said, "Determine the location where the flower roots are. Dig a small hole several feet deep and place pig intestines as fertilizer in the hole. Then fill the hole with soil again. The roots will gradually grow out from the fertilized area. To make peonies thrive, you don't need to fertilize with human waste; you must use pig intestines. This was indeed done. Around the vernal equinox, tender shoots emerged. A Tang Dynasty poem said, 'Green willows are suitable for making spring for two families.' Now it can be said that peonies are suitable for making spring for two families, as the roots emerge from under the garden wall." It was already winter, and this was done according to the method. The next year, there was no sign of anything. Qian said, "This method can be used again this winter, and it will definitely be effective." The following year, peony shoots from the neighboring garden sprouted out near the wall. Therefore, extra care was taken in nurturing them. After three years, they flourished. The flowers were as large as those in the neighboring garden. The owner of the neighboring garden invited people to admire the famous flowers. Yang also participated. As the banquet was about to end, Yang invited all the guests and the host, saying, "Tomorrow, I will honor you all with a visit to my garden to admire the peonies." Upon arrival, they saw that they were no different from the neighboring flowers. Everyone asked where they came from. The owner of the neighboring garden was particularly surprised. Yang smiled and said to the owner of the neighboring garden, "The famous flowers in your garden have revealed their spring splendor." He then told them about the root grafting method. The official changed a Song Dynasty poem to jest, "The spring colors fill the garden and cannot be contained; a branch comes out from under the wall." Everyone applauded and laughed.

A Stupid Ox Sold as a Coolie · Yà · Hún 231

My neighbor's son, surnamed Yu, was extremely dull. People commonly called him a "stupid ox." He would sometimes chirpily respond. Learning crafts and engaging in commerce, he was unable to complete any task. In the thirteenth year of the Republic, he went to Guangdong to live with his uncle. He disappeared in Guangdong in less than a month. For six or seven years, searches were conducted everywhere, but there were no signs. Everyone said that he was more likely to be dead than alive. Who knew that a month ago, this missing "stupid ox" had leisurely returned home? Everyone was astonished and quickly inquired about his whereabouts. According to the "ox," he had nothing to do at his uncle's place in Guangdong and spent his days wandering the streets. One day, he met a man on Jianglan Street. The man was luxuriously dressed and acted generously. Seeing him idly walking down the street, he used asking for directions as an excuse to exchange surnames and origins, including his clan and place of residence. The "ox" answered everything without hesitation. The man introduced himself as Qian Zaidong, a comprador on a certain ship with many workers under him. The "ox," feeling frustrated and looking for work, disregarded the potential dangers and pleaded for help. Qian agreed to arrange a position for him on the ship, with a certain amount of salary each month. He warned him not to reveal this opportunity to others to avoid being preempted. The "ox" respectfully agreed. They arranged to meet again at a teahouse the next day to discuss the matter further. The "ox" went as agreed, and Qian was already there. Qian said that the matter had been settled, but the ship was urgently sailing that day. If he wanted the job, he might as well board the ship with him right away. All his belongings could be taken care of after boarding. The "ox" was overjoyed, thinking that he was lucky to have met such a good person in this degenerate era. His gratitude was indescribable. He boarded a large ship with Qian. Qian told the "ox" to stay in the cabin and not come out. After some time, the ropes were untied, and the ship sailed. The "ox" searched everywhere for Qian but could not find him, which made him uneasy. At mealtime, he was called to eat by a ship worker. The ship sailed for a day and a night and arrived at a deserted island. The "ox" was driven ashore by a worker. The "ox" tried to reason and inquire, but he saw five or six people resembling workers on the shore, who seized him and dragged him into a mine. Despite shouting and screaming, no one helped him. From then on, he lived in darkness, living the life of a beast of burden. The supervisors were extremely cruel, and whipping was applied for the slightest rest. The suffering was unbearable. He thought of escaping, but there was no way out. He believed he would die in this mine. Unexpectedly, last year, during construction in the mine, the ore exploded, destroying the entire mine. Eight or nine out of ten workers were killed or injured, but the "ox" only suffered minor injuries. Four or five days after the mine explosion, a large ship came to the island to take away the surviving workers. The "ox" was among them. When the ship arrived in Hong Kong, although there was still supervision, the "ox" seized an opportunity and escaped, bearing his injuries. He begged his way to Guangdong and reached his uncle's place. He was given money to return home. He spoke with lingering fear. I have heard that there are gangs in Guangdong that sell coolies. The "ox" likely encountered one of them. I record this to warn young people who go to Guangdong.

Rustic Sayings from Bamboo Shoot Village · Zhī · Yuán 232

Fahua Mountain is located in Qinlü Township, on the main road to Liuxia Town. The beauty of West Lake converges here, so the area produces many mao bamboo. The shoots cast shadows, and the sound of their husks splitting can be heard. At the first spring thunder, bamboo shoots burst forth vigorously. However, mao bamboo shoots need to sprout in late spring. Villagers dig in the soil to find and cut them. They are no more than a foot long and are seasoned with Wu salt, making them tender and delicious. Even Su Dongpo's jade-like meditation food would have to take a back seat.

Mao bamboo shoots are also called cat bamboo shoots or cat's head bamboo shoots because their tips are pointed like cat ears. The counties of Yuhang, Lin'an, and Anji Xiaofeng near Hangzhou have dense bamboo forests and are major production areas. However, their shoots are either peeled of their outer skin, called bamboo shoot skin, or flattened and baked, called dried bamboo shoots. Their taste is inferior to those of Fahua. However, the ones produced in Fahua are best when they are first dug from the mountain. If they are transported overnight in baskets to the city, the husks will be dry and the flesh coarse, greatly diminishing their quality.

Fahua has an East Yue Temple. The temple has many Taoist priests who cultivate many bamboo mountains. If they are sent out with hoes and return with baskets, with the length and weight being just right, and with the aroma still lingering, paired with Lǐ'ān's [chef] dishes and the water shield soup from the Three Pools, the kitchen in the temple will have a flavor different from the mountain home. A word to meat-eaters: why not try it?

So she made a set of Chinese clothes, modeled after the palace attire of noble women of the Qing Dynasty. The upper garment was made of crepe and embroidered with Chinese characters. The lower garment was a pair of black satin trousers. The fit was perfect, and she was stunningly beautiful. Pauline deeply believed that this kind of clothing was ten thousand times better than Western clothes. She once said, "This dress is both beautiful and comfortable. I believe that among all kinds of clothes, this kind is the best." She wore this outfit several times in the "Female Pirate" film, which is currently showing at the Paris Opera House.

In recent months, Chen has created many more fine pieces, and the carved fan bones are all taken from famous calligraphies and paintings. His efforts are精劲, surpassing and entering the divine. It is now scheduled to be displayed at the Ningbo Tongxiang Association for a week starting on the 25th of this month. He will also provide stamps and rubbings of carved fans as gifts for guests. Publishing News: The scenery of West Lake is the best in the world. In recent years, material construction has been advancing rapidly. However, there is still a lack of literary publications to which the spirit of life is entrusted. Mr. Zhu Songjian, in view of this, gathered fellow literary artists in Hangzhou to organize the Xiling Literary Publishing House and publish the "Flowers on the Lake" magazine. The inaugural issue has now been published. The layout is novel, and the material is exquisite. It is truly a good companion for those who love literature and art. Major bookstores in Shanghai and Hangzhou all act as agents.

Common Sense Gleanings · Lǚ · Bīng 233

When we write in a sloping or slanting way, if we are not careful, the ink easily stains our clothes. If it is a new stain that is not dry, we should quickly use blotting paper to surround the stain and twist it tightly to absorb the ink. Then, take a soft cloth and dip it in a little tomato juice. Apply it from the edge to the center. Let it sit for a few minutes, then wash it off. If traces still appear, repeat the above method until it is completely clean.

If the ink stain has been there for a long time, the removal process is more troublesome. You can buy some oxalic acid from the pharmacy and dissolve it in water. The ratio of water to acid should be twelve to one. For stains on white clothes, use boiling water. For colored clothes, warm water is sufficient. After the water and acid have dissolved, take a soft cloth, soak it in the solution, and scrub the stain vigorously. It should gradually become clean. However, the original color of the clothes will inevitably be slightly affected. You can mix one part vinegar with twelve parts cold water and soak the clothes in the mixture to restore their original luster.

Warmth in the Heart (One) (Nine) (Nine) · Bāo · Tiān · Xiào 234

Chapter 11: Emerald Net and Pearl Hairpins, a Beauty Marries a Handsome Man; Green Chamber and Crimson Canopy, a Famous Courtesan Marries into a Notable Family

Zuo Shichen thought secretly, "...Star Uncle's wife... has always been known for her beauty... She is a woman of both talent and beauty... I remember that in that girls' school... she was known as the queen of the whole school... The position of emperor in the world can be abolished... but the name of queen is hard to remove..." As the saying goes, "Hot porridge is difficult to make into a dish, and a beautiful wife is difficult to make into a husband"... This saying has a lot of profound meaning... It's just a pity that Liu Xing Uncle's physique is not very healthy... and cannot help but give him cause for concern... But this is something that he is happy about... and said, "I also agree with you... to use the rewards gained from your hard work... to gain one or two commemorative precious items... to wear on your loved one's body... what a pleasant and comforting thing that is..." Liu Xing Uncle listened very contentedly and said, "I am of this principle... Achievement is of this principle... Yesterday one of our relatives... he runs a jewelry store on Sanma Road... had two items... he persuaded me to buy... He said they were brought by a Nanyang merchant... Because there are other business matters... these two items can be sold without making money from others... Sold at cost... Two items... actually sold for one thousand two hundred dollars... For them who do jewelry business... this is just a small transaction..." Zuo Shichen asked him, "What are these two items?" Liu Xing Uncle said, "A jadeite necklace... to be sold for seven hundred dollars... Originally this kind of thing... is sold to foreign firms... foreign women... their clothes have no collars... to show off their white necks... so they often wear various necklaces... of course, the most luxurious... a string of perfectly round pearl necklaces... valued at tens of thousands... or even hundreds of thousands... Next is jadeite... but color and size... have a great relationship... However, Western women especially like jadeite necklaces... because the beads blend with the flesh tone... a string of green jadeite adorns a snow-white neck... how beautiful is that..." Because foreign women like to wear necklaces... if they don't have precious ones... they wear coral or amber necklaces... the lowest kind... are fake... But they told me... jadeite is sure to become very expensive in the future... The price this year... and the price of previous years is very different... This string of jadeite necklaces... is because it was brought by a guest from Nanyang... he still priced it in Nanyang... Nanyang is the concentration of jadeite... and he declared that he would not make money on it... seven hundred dollars is really not expensive... The other is a beaded phoenix... the beads are not very big... but small and round... the brilliance is also very good... that beaded phoenix is priced at five hundred dollars... the two items... belong to one person... they are both from that Nanyang guest... his intention is to sell the two items... together... if you only want one of them... he will have to add to this price..." My relative... he advised me to buy both items together... He said that jadeite gets more expensive every year... If you don't like it... after another three years... at least this string of jadeite necklaces... will be worth one thousand dollars..."

Gold Standard Rebounds by Three Taels and Eight Qian 236

Market Wave Gradually Calms, Signs of Rise: Yesterday, the turbulent situation in the gold standard market began to calm, and prices rebounded. Afternoon Closing Rises to 19 Taels and 1 Qian, then Suddenly HSBC Purchases Spot British Gold at 9 Pence and 8125: The market immediately showed vigor, and with a shortage of sellers, prices soared, increasing by 2 taels and several qian, reaching 19 taels at 11:30 AM. American Cotton Weekend Statistics Favor Shorts 246

New York, May 23rd, reports on the cotton market for the week: At the beginning of the week, the cotton market rose due to wind and storm damage to new cotton in the West and Central regions. However, it soon fell back as the weather turned sunny. Shorts bought in when the July futures price fell back. The position of the new cotton will become more active as the season progresses. The West and Central regions have been significantly damaged by excessive rainfall, and will likely need to be replanted. However, the rain in the East has been beneficial. Cotton fields in Georgia, Mitchell, Shelby Basin, and Texas have weeds, except for in the West and Northwest. However, labor and seeds in these states are sufficient for replanting. The weather has been poor this month, so many people have sold new cotton. However, the poor conditions before June are expected to recover, and good soil will allow new cotton to grow quickly next month.

Grain Rice Market Downriver Sales Stagnant and Lacking Vigor 250

White Jing, High Quality Fixed, Secondary Falls, Bian Yuan Also Declines

The amount of goods arriving at Zhabei yesterday was still sparse, with around 80 boats in the river. Market sales were very sluggish. Northern Jiangsu high-quality japonica rice barely maintained its original price, with prices around 21 yuan in the inner area. There was no apparent increase or decrease in the surface prices of medium-quality rice, but buyers actually had to reduce prices by nearly 10 cents. In addition, no one inquired about aged japonica rice priced below 19 yuan, further weakening transactions. Currently, northern and southern Jiangsu Pingmi rice are being sold by various stores on behalf of the suppliers, so the future of the japonica market is unlikely to recover. Thin indica rice sales are sluggish, and arrivals are also infrequent. Prices are stable. Sheep's Du and Pointed rice shipments are very small. A few boats carrying this product arrived in port in the past two days. Sales of this product are not smooth, but because the base is solid, the overall price is still set at 18 yuan and 56 cents for ordinary goods. Bian Yuan continues to be seen, but buying interest is declining, and prices are falling steadily. The market fell another 10 cents yesterday, showing a lack of vigor.

More than ten boats arrived at the South Shanghai West Road and South Road. Sales on this street are flat. There is still some Changshu and Wuxi high-quality japonica rice being sold in small quantities. Prices remain high at 20 yuan, but the market is neither prosperous nor declining. Suzhou Tongli and other machine-milled japonica rice are being procured by rural villages, so the market is stable. However, all transactions are small and scattered. Wholesale goods are stagnant because Chongming, Tongzhou, and Haizhou merchants are taking a wait-and-see approach. Sales of early-season thin indica rice in South Road focus on high-quality rice. It is difficult for ordinary secondary goods to develop. Moreover, sources are closer than others, and the market is softening by nearly a foot. Sheep's Du and Pointed rice have recently arrived in port and are more popular than in the North City. Sales are also not weak. However, the unstable prices of imported rice currently affect this rice, and prices are sometimes reduced. Ordinary goods are priced around 18 yuan, and the arrival of Bian Yuan is very small. Interest is slightly moving, but the overall price is slightly lower due to poor conditions in Zhabei.

Recent Flour Squeezed to 60 Cents Outside the Customs 251

Forward contracts have all fallen back

The flour market suddenly showed signs of chaos yesterday. Due to the transition between old and new wheat this month, and the unwillingness of manufacturers to maintain prices, manipulators took advantage of the situation, repeatedly squeezing shorts and raising prices. Yesterday, the market saw bulls not only unwilling to loosen their grip, but also increasing prices and buying in, so the highest price squeezed to 2 taels, 6 qian, 0 li and 7.5 hao. This exceeded the bull's target of 60 cents. Compared to yesterday's closing price, it rose by 3 cents for no reason. When the near-term prices were at their highest, the prices of forward contracts also rose. However, later, because the weather was very good, with plenty of sunshine, inland bulls sold off one after another. All contracts from June onwards saw a decline. If the weather continues to be good during the wheat harvest, and the annual food supply is stably harvested, then the sentiment will not be as strong as it is now, and the opportunity for the market to fall back should begin. As a result, this month's price rose by 2 fen and 2 li and 5 hao compared to before. June to August contracts fell by 7 li and 5 hao, and September and October contracts each fell by 1 fen and 2 li and 5 hao.

Wheat Market Shows Slightly Softening Signs 252

Yesterday, the wheat futures market generally showed flat and weak signs. Because the weather is good and the price of imported wheat is also slightly lower by 2, 3, 5, or 60 cents, the market sentiment is weak. However, the key to this will be the weather at the time of the new wheat harvest. If the weather is good and the annual food supply is stably harvested, then the sentiment will not be as strong and unyielding as it is now. As a result, June, July, and October contracts each fell slightly by 1 fen compared to the previous day, and August and October contracts remained unchanged. Arrivals of spot wheat have been light, and the mills are neither too close nor too far. Given the recent tight flour situation, spot goods can temporarily hold steady. However, as the new wheat season approaches, the mills will relax their grip, and old goods will have to be discounted. A shipment of Xuzhou wheat, Suzhou wheat, and Qingjiangpu wheat, medium to good quality, opened at 5 taels and 1 qian, and high-quality goods opened at 5 taels and 1 qian and 5 fen, totaling 2,000 bags, and were purchased by Fuxin.

New Rapeseed Vigorously Purchased by Foreign Firms 253

This year's new rapeseed crop is better than in previous years. Various producing areas have been shipping to Shanghai one after another, so foreign firms are gradually paying attention. Currently, shipments arriving in Shanghai include Hankou, Jiujiang, Wenzhou, and Taizhou goods. Among them, Wenzhou goods are the most numerous, and the rest are small shipments. Initial sales in Shanghai were only slightly active on this street. Due to the lack of a formal market price, foreign firms vigorously purchased yesterday, buying 500 bags of Wenzhou goods for 2 years at a price of 6 taels, 1 qian, and 8 fen.

Jida Organizes Specimen Collection Group 259

Those who study biology value the collection of specimens first, and then research can be verified and progress made. Therefore, researchers in Europe and the United States spend years collecting specimens, traveling around the world, and their spirit is admirable. Therefore, they must make contributions every year to help the world evolve. For example, on the question of "whether humans evolved from apes," they have collected specimens. The Department of Biology of Jinan University, in view of this, has specially organized a specimen collection group to depart for North China, and then to the Northwest and Northeast. The scope of the collection is quite large, including all stone age human, monkey and animal skulls, and the strange animals and plants of each region are included. The deadline is set for September. Earlier, the president of the school submitted a request to the National Government to order protection in various provinces, so there is absolutely no danger to the safety of the group. The group was originally scheduled to depart last month, but was delayed until now due to funding issues. It was only recently that the school authorities provided a large amount of funding to make the trip possible. The group is divided into two departments: the Guidance Department, with Li Guochang as the general director, Professors Gao Zhongkui and Xu Renji as plant guides, Liu Zengyao and Huang Nong as animal guides, and Li Xiqi and two technicians as managers; and the Affairs Department, with Cai Guoping, Zhang Hanwen, Huang Guoping, Lin Yaoting, Liao Chunhua, and student Huang Bingquan as members. The collection subgroups are assigned temporarily. This is the first time that the school has opened a Chinese biological collection group, and the results will be remarkable in the future. It is hoped that other universities can learn from the school and that all departments should have practical experiments. (Wubujing)

Sunday (5)

Act Two of The Merchant of Venice

After Seeing "The Merchant of Venice" · Zheng · Yong 260

The long-awaited "Merchant of Venice" finally premiered on the 17th.

The Drama Association's performance of "The Merchant of Venice" this time, had been in preparation for several months. The very long play has more than thirty actors, so it must be said that the arrangement and the number of actors presented difficulties. The result of this performance is that the performance on stage and the plot in the book are about the same. The actors also achieved considerable proficiency. This is admirable and cannot be denied as progress.

The entire play of "The Merchant of Venice" is divided into five acts. The main characters in these five acts are Portia, Bassanio, Antonio, Shylock, and his daughter Jessica. The status of each protagonist, the personality of each person, the tone of voice when speaking, and the attitude of showing joy and sorrow, must each be appropriate, so that no one is slightly deficient. This will ultimately bring the entire "Merchant of Venice" from the script to the stage to vividly express it. Although the actors who played these few people were passable, the one who left the deepest impression on the audience was Shen Tongjun as Shylock, who fully manifested his cunning and cruel nature, bringing misfortune to others and misfortune to himself. However, Shylock's frantic expression when he searched everywhere for his daughter Jessica after she eloped should not be too busy and agitated. The sound of calling his daughter should be implicit, sad, and breathless. Also, Shylock's stubborn and vicious attitude towards the inquisitor in the Venetian court in the first scene of the fourth act, expressing his anger and wanting to vent his inner hatred, the only thing is revenge on Antonio, and the posture of cutting a pound of flesh and the trembling language, are very vivid. It can be said that this is the most outstanding part of the entire play.

Mr. Huang Yimei, who played Antonio, was also able to portray the loyalty of a merchant to his friend Bassanio, but his movements were a bit slow. However, in terms of the plot, it was not very inferior.

Miss Portia's beautiful appearance, in Yu Xiuyun,

Page 26

May 25, 1930 (Shen Bao Local Supplement) Sunday (6)

The lady's clever figure, clear and white face, and very clear voice are very appropriate. Her graceful posture and dignified aristocratic demeanor are especially praised by the audience. Ms. Yu is indeed an important and indispensable role in the play.

Regarding the scenery, too much precious time was spent, because the scenery was too slow, causing the audience to be unable to maintain the patience of keeping quiet, causing the audience to make noise and talk, thus destroying the silent atmosphere in the performance hall, or some meaningless arbitrary coughs and sputum sounds. (If the curtain opens quickly, there will naturally be fewer of these phenomena.) As for the scene in Portia's house in the second act, the arrangement is not very good, and it will change into something like a civilized play in the Great World. In other words, the furnishings in Portia's house must be rich and beautiful, but they must not be too close to vulgarity, or even get too bad. Because of too much attention to realism, it becomes complicated and inelegant. The scenery set in the garden of Portia's house at the end of the play is still quite appropriate. The green shade forest is really not easy to make well on the stage. It is a pity that the color brought by the lights is too heavy, and the green does not look like the bright silver light at night. This point seems to be more appropriate to use blue, and the color should be lighter. Although these are very small things, for the sake of perfection, I can't help but nitpick. But the light and shadow in the previous acts have to be said to be very appropriate. There is also one thing that is very satisfactory, that is, everyone in the audience this time was very able to strictly maintain order, which is a rare quietness compared to the usual performances in the drama club. It seems that the artistic skills on the stage can very much stimulate the audience's brains.

Physical Education of Guanghua Female Students 261

The physical education of Guanghua female students is very immature, because since the enrollment of female students, the number of days has been very small, and the various facilities are not yet complete. Most of the female students, in addition to attending classes every day, are neatly dressed and walk around on the playground and the road, without any sports achievements. If this continues, it will really fail the expectations of the female students. The school authorities, in view of this, opened up a corner in the northeast as a sports field for female students, and hired a certain female physical educator as a professor. Recently, a volleyball team was organized, and a certain teacher from a middle school was invited to be the instructor. Every morning, dozens of "red scarf team" heroes can be seen walking to and from the playground in a majestic manner. This may be the beginning of physical education for Guanghua female students.

However, there is one thing that most hinders their physical development, that is, whenever female students do gymnastics, male students, like a tide, surround them in several layers to watch from the sidelines. Saying "good" is not good. Shouting loudly, "Her hair is too loose," "She has pigeon toes," the criticism can be described as "meticulous." The female students are a little embarrassed and afraid of going to physical education, so many people do not attend class. Fortunately, the physical education department has enclosed the female students' playground with a fence, leaving only one small entrance and exit. It is said that there are two purposes for this: one is to prevent male students from watching, and the other is to work hard to practice physical education. (Four)

New Discoveries in the Excavation of Anyang Yinxu

Newly unearthed divination bone, the belly of the tortoise shell has been shaved and the carving is very meticulous. The clay has not been completely removed. There is a small hole near the top, possibly for installation purposes.

The ceramic pattern on the bronze ritual vessel is derived from the Shang Dynasty Yi vessels. The patterns are all small pieces, and there is Guan Xun Yi Fan along the edge, which can be used several times. When casting the vessel, if several molds can form one vessel, some will be wrapped in copper rust.

A picture of the excavation scene. The workers either dig the soil with small shovels or crawl with their five fingers. Even small objects are completely taken out without damaging them with water. Mr. Li Xu is the supervisor.

Rope-patterned rice

Animal-eared white pottery. These types of pottery are all fragments in the soil, without sound or shape, but the carved patterns are extremely rich, or they are also types of Yi vessels.

There are round feet under the earthenware pot. They came out at seven o'clock, already late.

Newly unearthed bone treasure engraved with characters. It is a live shoulder blade that has been shaved. There are words (Liao Shi Ju Shui) in the engraved words, which is today's water. There are extremely many place names in the bone inscriptions, and only this water can be accurately written down now.

The purpose of the carved bone chips is unknown. Some are inlaid with turquoise, and some seem to be decorations.

Bronze spear unearthed. Looking at the image, ancient weapons unearthed are mostly halberds, and spears are very rare. The bottom of this spear is empty to receive the secret. It is undoubtedly a stabbing weapon, and the state of preservation is very good, and the edge is as new.

The Institute of History and Philology of the Academia Sinica of the Republic of China is excavating the Yin Ruins in Anyang, Henan. It is still a major undertaking in the modern academic world in China. Recently, Mr. Zi Qingzhi, the director of the Ancient Group and Anyang Excavation, passed through Shanghai on official business and talked about the excavation and color photography, saying that since the oracle bone inscriptions were unearthed in Guangxu, they have been collected by Wang (Yi Rong), Liu (E), Luo (Zhenyu), and edited by Sun (Yirang) and Wang (Guowei), becoming an important issue in the Chinese academic world. However, the institute focused on this matter in the 30 years of the Republic of China, only seeking to replicate this matter from the perspective of the box-stone school. It devoted itself to this and achieved nothing other than textual research. Important materials are therefore grouped by year. This cannot be compared to Mr. Dong Zuobin. China has always regarded archaeology as inferior work and disdains to do it. But the importance of ancient objects only lies in their characters. When the institute organized archaeological affairs, it immediately corrected this point of view and took excavation as the basic work of archaeology. The first time it was implemented in Yinxu, Anyang, was in the autumn of the 17th year, and the spring and autumn of the 18th year continued for two times. Each time, there were important discoveries. The research station then published a special issue by the Institute of History and Philology. In total, the three excavations achieved the most important things regarding the following common points: (1) The scope of the Yin Ruins; (2) The situation of the accumulation of each layer in the ground; (3) The changes in the map after the formation of the region; (4) The discovery of new oracle bone inscriptions and their accumulating conditions; (5) Simultaneous evidence of oracle bone inscriptions. The most important of these is the Tao, stone, carved jade, bone, and bronze vessels of various kinds. Regarding the above questions and discoveries, there are specialized texts and discussions that will be published in the Anyang excavation report one after another. The excavation work is not yet fully completed, so the institute has four more excavation plans. When the time is right, the team will set off immediately. Mr. Zi also said that according to the experience gained from the discoveries, the oracle bone inscriptions currently stored in the market, various museums, and private collections have been published and engraved. Among them, the oracle bone inscriptions discovered by the Institute of History and Philology of the Academia Sinica, which were examined with a scientific eye, are the only species of genuine products. Although the current number is only more than 3,000 pieces, their value is higher than all the oracle bone inscriptions currently stored in various places.

Visiting relatives - Ms. Li Dandan, who became famous for starring in the film "Mulan Joins the Army," has been studying literature in the United Kingdom for many years. She recently returned to her hometown for vacation and arrived in Shanghai on the Guqi Maru 9. She will have to go to Europe again after a month.

Famous object - A photo of the famous actor Mei Lanfang and the American playwright and director Belareo. The cup held by Mei is what Napoleon and Josephine used when they got married. Mr. Bellareo got it at a high price more than ten years ago.
